    SELECT [o0].[OrderDetailID], [o0].[OrderID], [o0].[Price], [o0].[ProductID], [o0].[Quantity], [p].[ProductID] AS [ProductID0], [p].[CategoryID], [p].[Price] AS [Price0], [p].[ProductImagePath], [p].[ProductName], [p].[Stock]
    FROM [orderdetails] AS [o0]
    LEFT JOIN [products] AS [p] ON [o0].[ProductID] = [p].[ProductID]
) AS [s] ON [o].[OrderID] = [s].[OrderID]
WHERE [o].[UserID] = @userId
ORDER BY [o].[OrderID], [s].[OrderDetailID]
